Bit coded\-: 0 set -\/-\/$>$ simulation not stopped, 1 set -\/-\/$>$ simulation paused, 2 set -\/-\/$>$ real-\/time switch on, 3-\/5\-: edit mode type (0=no edit mode, 1=triangle, 2=vertex, 3=edge, 4=path, 5=U\-I) $\ast$/
